The copies of the records for which this certification is made are true and complete reproductions of the original records that are maintained at King’s Daughters’ Health.

The original records were made in the regular course of business, and it was in the regular course of business that King’s Daughters’ Health made these records at or during the time that the

patient was cared for at the Hospital or in any of its wholly owned, healthcare settings.

This certification is authorized by Jim Nichols, custodian of the billing records.
